<s> although use of the metric system has been sanctioned by law in the us since 1866 it has been slow in displacing the american adaptation of the british imperial system known as the us customary system <\s>
<s> the us is the only industrialized nation that does not mainly use the metric system in its commercial and standards activities but there is increasing acceptance in science medicine government and many sectors of industry <\s>
